class="fusion-inline-sep">|</span></p><div class="fusion-content-sep sep-shadow" style="border-color:#ffffff;"></div><div class="fusion-post-content-container"><p>The Black Moon is a virtual astrological point, which represents the lunar apogee. I will refer to it as Black Moon Lilith (BML) in this article, to differentiate it from other astrological points (such as the asteroid Lilith or the Dark Moon). The apogee is the point in the Moon\xe2\x80\x99s elliptical orbit around the Earth at which it is furthest away from the Earth. It is at this position that it almost escapes, but doesn\'t! </p></div></div><div class="fusion-meta-info"><div class="fusion-alignleft"><a class="fusion-read-more" sep-shadow" style="border-color:#ffffff;"></div><div class="fusion-post-content-container"><p>The Black Moon is a virtual astrological point, which represents the lunar apogee.
